--- GENERATED EVIDENCE RULES PROMPT ---
You must enforce the following strict evidence validation rules per company policy.

If any rule fails, immediately set `evidence_standard_met` to `false`.

2. [RULE: REQ_GENERAL_OBJECT_PART] for claims involving 'general claim review':
 - MANDATE: The claimed object and relevant part should be visible clearly enough to inspect the claimed condition.
 - FAILURE CONDITION: If the submitted visual evidence is blurry, obscured, missing from the frame, or taken from an unreadable distance/angle, this requirement is NOT satisfied.

3. [RULE: REQ_GENERAL_MULTI_IMAGE] for claims involving 'multi-image rows':
 - MANDATE: Each submitted image should be considered separately; at least one relevant image should show the claimed object or part clearly enough to evaluate the claim.
 - FAILURE CONDITION: If the submitted visual evidence is blurry, obscured, missing from the frame, or taken from an unreadable distance/angle, this requirement is NOT satisfied.

4. [RULE: REQ_CAR_BODY_PANEL] for claims involving 'dent or scratch':
 - MANDATE: The claimed car panel or bumper should be visible from an angle where surface marks or deformation can be assessed.
 - FAILURE CONDITION: If the submitted visual evidence is blurry, obscured, missing from the frame, or taken from an unreadable distance/angle, this requirement is NOT satisfied.

5. [RULE: REQ_CAR_GLASS_LIGHT_MIRROR] for claims involving 'crack, broken, or missing part':
 - MANDATE: The claimed glass, light, mirror, or component should be visible clearly enough to inspect cracks, breakage, or missing parts.
 - FAILURE CONDITION: If the submitted visual evidence is blurry, obscured, missing from the frame, or taken from an unreadable distance/angle, this requirement is NOT satisfied.

6. [RULE: REQ_CAR_IDENTITY_OR_SIDE] for claims involving 'vehicle identity or orientation':
 - MANDATE: When the claim depends on vehicle identity, side, or orientation, the image set should show enough context to match the claimed vehicle and part.
 - FAILURE CONDITION: If the submitted visual evidence is blurry, obscured, missing from the frame, or taken from an unreadable distance/angle, this requirement is NOT satisfied.

7. [RULE: REQ_REVIEW_TRUST] for claims involving 'reviewability':
 - MANDATE: The submitted images should provide visual evidence that is usable, relevant to the claim, and grounded in the claimed object.
 - FAILURE CONDITION: If the submitted visual evidence is blurry, obscured, missing from the frame, or taken from an unreadable distance/angle, this requirement is NOT satisfied.
